[38;2;255;255;255m⏺[39m [1mRoot Cause Analysis[22m

  [1mTASK_COMPLETE[22m

  The program crashes due to a [1mNULL pointer dereference[22m in the [38;2;177;185;249madd_score[39m
  function at line 26 in [38;2;177;185;249mdemo-buggy.c[39m.

  [1mRoot Cause:[22m
  - The [38;2;177;185;249mStudent[39m structure has a [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m field that points to a dynamically
  allocated array
  - When the student is created, the [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m field is initialized to [38;2;177;185;249mNULL[39m
  (0x0000000000000000)
  - The [38;2;177;185;249madd_score[39m function attempts to write to [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[s->num_scores][39m
  without checking if [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m is NULL
  - This causes a segmentation fault when trying to write to memory address
   0x0

  [1mCrash Details:[22m
  - [1mLocation:[22m [38;2;177;185;249mdemo-buggy.c:26:30[39m in [38;2;177;185;249madd_score(Student *s, float score)[39m
  - [1mCode:[22m [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[s->num_scores] = score;[39m
  - [1mError:[22m EXC_BAD_ACCESS (code=1, address=0x0)
  - [1mStudent state:[22m name="Alice", age=20, scores=NULL, num_scores=0
  - [1mAttempted score:[22m 95.5

  [1mFix Required:[22m
  The [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m array needs to be allocated before use, either in the student
  creation function or at the beginning of [38;2;177;185;249madd_score[39m.
